<script type="module">
import { initializeApp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.0/firebase-app.js";
import { getFirestore, collection, getDocs, addDoc, onSnapshot, orderBy, query, where, Timestamp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.12.0/firebase-firestore.js";

const firebaseConfig = {
apiKey: "AIzaSyAyxBcBBypSrspnc_5RcLmhR2RuVwPa5ZQ",
authDomain: "pass-instant.firebaseapp.com",
projectId: "pass-instant",
storageBucket: "pass-instant.firebasestorage.app",
messagingSenderId: "234758483474",
appId: "1:234758483474:web:7d739963a99a7bd573f2cb"
};

const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
const db = getFirestore(app);

// ── Charger les partenaires depuis Firestore ──
async function loadPartenaires() {
try {
const snap = await getDocs(collection(db, 'partenaires'));
if (!snap.empty) {
window.PARTNERS = [];
snap.forEach(doc => {
window.PARTNERS.push({ id: doc.id, ...doc.data() });
});
console.log(`✅ ${window.PARTNERS.length} partenaires chargés depuis Firebase`);
renderList();
} else {
console.log('ℹ️ Aucun partenaire dans Firebase, utilisation des données de démo');
seedDemoData();
}
} catch(e) {
console.log('⚠️ Erreur Firebase:', e.message, '— données de démo utilisées');
}
}

// ── Écouter les offres flash en temps réel ──
function listenFlash() {
try {
const q = query(collection(db, 'offres_flash'), where('active', '==', true));
onSnapshot(q, snap => {
const flashData = {};
snap.forEach(doc => {
const d = doc.data();
flashData[d.partenaire_id] = { titre: d.titre, desc: d.details || '', timer: d.expire_dans };
});
// Mettre à jour les offres flash dans PARTNERS
if (window.PARTNERS) {
window.PARTNERS.forEach(p => {
p.flash = flashData[p.id] || null;
});
// Rafraîchir l'affichage si on est sur accueil ou flash
const activeScr = document.querySelector('.scr.on');
if (activeScr) {
const id = activeScr.id.replace('scr-', '');
if (id === 'flash') renderFlash();
if (id === 'partenaires') renderList();
}
// Mettre à jour le point rouge sur Flash
const hasFlash = Object.keys(flashData).length > 0;
document.querySelectorAll('.ndot').forEach(d => d.style.display = hasFlash ? 'block' : 'none');
}
});
} catch(e) {
console.log('⚠️ Écoute flash impossible:', e.message);
}
}

// ── Publier une offre flash depuis l'interface partenaire ──
window.publierOffre = async function() {
const titre = document.getElementById('pub-titre').value.trim();
const details = document.getElementById('pub-details').value.trim();
const timer = document.querySelector('.dp.on')?.textContent || '2h';
if (!titre) { alert('Veuillez saisir un titre pour votre offre.'); return; }
try {
await addDoc(collection(db, 'offres_flash'), {
partenaire_id: 'baiesomme-evasion',
partenaire_nom: 'Baie de Somme Évasion',
titre, details,
expire_dans: timer,
active: true,
created_at: Timestamp.now()
});
goTo('confirmation');
} catch(e) {
console.log('Erreur publication:', e.message);
goTo('confirmation'); // On affiche quand même la confirmation
}
};

// ── Insérer les données de démo dans Firebase (1ère fois) ──
async function seedDemoData() {
console.log('🌱 Insertion des données de démo dans Firebase...');
const demo = window.PARTNERS_DEMO || [];
for (const p of demo) {
try {
await addDoc(collection(db, 'partenaires'), p);
} catch(e) { console.log('Erreur seed:', e.message); }
}
loadPartenaires();
}

// Lancer au démarrage
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
// Sauvegarder les données de démo comme fallback
window.PARTNERS_DEMO = window.PARTNERS ? [...window.PARTNERS] : [];
loadPartenaires();
listenFlash();
});
</script>

// Langue active
let lang = localStorage.getItem('lang') || navigator.language.substring(0,2) || 'fr';
if (!['fr','en','nl','de'].includes(lang)) lang = 'fr';
function t(key) { return T[lang][key] || T['fr'][key] || key; }

window.setLang = function(l) {
lang = l;
localStorage.setItem('lang', l);
applyTranslations();
renderList();
renderFlash();
document.querySelectorAll('.lang-btn').forEach(b => {
b.classList.toggle('on', b.dataset.lang === l);
});
};

function applyTranslations() {
// Accueil
document.querySelectorAll('[data-t]').forEach(el => {
const key = el.dataset.t;
if (key) el.textContent = t(key);
});
document.querySelectorAll('[data-t-ph]').forEach(el => {
el.placeholder = t(el.dataset.tPh);
});
}

function getZones(){return[{id:'all',label:t('all_zones')},{id:'albatre',label:t('zone_albatre')},{id:'baiesomme',label:t('zone_baiesomme')},{id:'authie',label:t('zone_authie')},{id:'vallee',label:t('zone_vallee')}];}
function getCats(){return[{id:'all',label:t('all_cats')},{id:'restauration',label:t('cat_restauration'),ico:'<path d="M18 8h1a4 4 0 010 8h-1M2 8h16v9a4 4 0 01-4 4H6a4 4 0 01-4-4V8zM6 1v3M10 1v3M14 1v3"/>'},{id:'nature',label:t('cat_nature'),ico:'<path d="M12 22V12M12 12C12 7 7 3 3 3c0 5 3 9 9 9zM12 12c0-5 5-9 9-9-1 5-4 9-9 9"/>'},{id:'commerces',label:t('cat_commerces'),ico:'<path d="M6 2L3 6v14a2 2 0 002 2h14a2 2 0 002-2V6l-3-4zM3 6h18M16 10a4 4 0 01-8 0"/>'},{id:'insolite',label:t('cat_insolite'),ico:'<polygon points="12 2 15.09 8.26 22 9.27 17 14.14 18.18 21.02 12 17.77 5.82 21.02 7 14.14 2 9.27 8.91 8.26 12 2"/>'},{id:'indoor',label:t('cat_indoor'),ico:'<rect x="3" y="3" width="18" height="18" rx="2"/><path d="M9 9h6M9 13h6M9 17h4"/>'},{id:'bienetre',label:t('cat_bienetre'),ico:'<path d="M20.84 4.61a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 0L12 5.67l-1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 7.78l1.06 1.06L12 21.23l7.78-7.78 1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 000-7.78z"/>'},{id:'voyageur',label:t('cat_voyageur'),ico:'<circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"/><path d="M12 8v4l3 3"/>'},{id:'bonus',label:t('cat_bonus'),ico:'<circle cx="12" cy="8" r="6"/><path d="M12 14l-4 8h8l-4-8z"/>'}];}
const PARTNERS=[
{id:1,name:'Baie de Somme Évasion',cat:'nature',zone:'baiesomme',avantage:'10% de réduction sur toutes les sorties',dist:0.8,coords:[50.186,1.642],flash:{titre:'2 places en pirogue disponibles !',desc:'Départ ce soir à 18h30.',timer:'2h'}},

const HOR=[['Lundi','9h – 18h'],['Mardi','9h – 18h'],['Mercredi','9h – 18h'],['Jeudi','9h – 18h'],['Vendredi','9h – 20h'],['Samedi','8h – 20h'],['Dimanche','8h – 18h']];
const JIDX=[6,0,1,2,3,4,5];
let aCat='all',aZone='all',sortDist=true,prevScr='partenaires';

function goTo(id){
document.querySelectorAll('.scr').forEach(s=>s.classList.remove('on'));
document.querySelectorAll('.nav').forEach(n=>n.remove && 0);
document.getElementById('scr-'+id).classList.add('on');
if(id==='confirmation') startCounters();
if(id==='flash') renderFlash();
if(id==='partenaires') renderList();
if(id==='carte') setTimeout(initCarte,100);
window.scrollTo(0,0);
}
function goBack(){goTo(prevScr);}
function filterCat(cat){aCat=cat;goTo('partenaires');setTimeout(()=>{buildCats();renderList();},50);}
function showFiche(id){
prevScr=document.querySelector('.scr.on').id.replace('scr-','');
const p=PARTNERS.find(x=>x.id===id);if(!p)return;
const CATS=getCats();const ZONES=getZones();const cat=CATS.find(c=>c.id===p.cat)||CATS[0];
const zone=ZONES.find(z=>z.id===p.zone)||ZONES[0];
window._ficheId=id;
document.getElementById('fiche-ico').innerHTML=cat.ico||'';
document.getElementById('fiche-name').textContent=p.name;
document.getElementById('fiche-cat').textContent=cat.label;
document.getElementById('fiche-zone').textContent=zone.label+' · '+p.dist+' km de vous';
document.getElementById('fiche-avantage').textContent=p.avantage;
document.getElementById('fiche-adresse').innerHTML=p.name+'<br><span class="muted">À '+p.dist+' km de vous</span>';
const fe=document.getElementById('fiche-flash'),fb=document.getElementById('fiche-btn-flash');
if(p.flash){fe.style.display='block';fb.style.display='block';document.getElementById('fiche-flash-title').textContent=p.flash.titre;document.getElementById('fiche-flash-desc').textContent=p.flash.desc;document.getElementById('fiche-flash-timer').textContent='Expire dans '+p.flash.timer;}
else{fe.style.display='none';fb.style.display='none';}
const td=JIDX[new Date().getDay()];
document.getElementById('fiche-horaires').innerHTML=HOR.map((h,i)=>`<div class="hr${i===td?' today':''}"><span class="j">${h[0]}${i===td?" (aujourd'hui)":''}</span><span class="h">${h[1]}</span></div>`).join('');
goTo('fiche');
}
function renderList(){
buildZones();buildCats();
const q=(document.getElementById('search')||{value:''}).value.toLowerCase().trim();
let f=PARTNERS.filter(p=>(aCat==='all'||p.cat===aCat)&&(aZone==='all'||p.zone===aZone)&&(!q||p.name.toLowerCase().includes(q)||p.avantage.toLowerCase().includes(q)));
if(sortDist)f.sort((a,b)=>a.dist-b.dist);else f.sort((a,b)=>a.name.localeCompare(b.name));
document.getElementById('count').textContent=t('partner_count')(f.length);
const zm=Object.fromEntries(getZones().map(z=>[z.id,z.label]));
const CATS2=getCats();const cm=Object.fromEntries(CATS2.map(c=>[c.id,{l:c.label,i:c.ico||''}]));
document.getElementById('list').innerHTML=f.length?f.map(p=>`
<div class="pc${p.flash?' fl':''}" onclick="showFiche(${p.id})">
<div class="pt"><div class="pico"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--mm)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round">${cm[p.cat]?.i||''}</svg></div>
<div class="pi"><div class="pn">${p.name}</div><div class="pm"><span class="pcat">${cm[p.cat]?.l||''}</span><span class="sep">·</span><span class="pzt"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21 10c0 7-9 13-9 13s-9-6-9-13a9 9 0 0118 0z"/><circle cx="12" cy="10" r="3"/></svg>${zm[p.zone]||''}</span></div>
<div class="pav">${p.avantage}</div>${p.flash?`<div class="pfb"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M13 2L3 14h9l-1 8 10-12h-9l1-8z"/></svg>${p.flash.titre}</div>`:''}
</div><div class="pdist">${p.dist} km</div></div></div>`).join(''):'<div class="empty">Aucun partenaire trouvé</div>';
}
function renderFlash(){
const f=PARTNERS.filter(p=>p.flash);
const zm=Object.fromEntries(getZones().map(z=>[z.id,z.label]));
document.getElementById('flash-list').innerHTML=f.length?f.map(p=>`
<div class="fc" onclick="showFiche(${p.id})"><div class="fc-top"><div class="fbadge"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M13 2L3 14h9l-1 8 10-12h-9l1-8z"/></svg>FLASH</div><div class="ftimer">Expire dans ${p.flash.timer}</div></div>
<div class="fttl">${p.flash.titre}</div><div class="fpar">${p.name}</div>
<div class="fzone"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M21 10c0 7-9 13-9 13s-9-6-9-13a9 9 0 0118 0z"/><circle cx="12" cy="10" r="3"/></svg>${zm[p.zone]} · ${p.dist} km</div></div>`).join(''):'<div class="empty">Aucune offre flash en ce moment</div>';
}
function buildZones(){const ZONES=getZones();document.getElementById('zone-filters').innerHTML=ZONES.map(z=>`<div class="pill zone${z.id===aZone?' on':''}" onclick="setZone('${z.id}')">${z.label}</div>`).join('');}
function buildCats(){const CATS=getCats();document.getElementById('cat-filters').innerHTML=CATS.map(c=>`<div class="pill${c.id===aCat?' on':''}" onclick="setCat('${c.id}')">${c.label}</div>`).join('');}
function setZone(id){aZone=id;buildZones();renderList();}
function setCat(id){aCat=id;buildCats();renderList();}
function toggleSort(){sortDist=!sortDist;document.getElementById('sort-label').textContent=sortDist?'Distance':'Alphabétique';renderList();}
function setType(el){document.querySelectorAll('.tc').forEach(c=>c.classList.remove('on'));el.classList.add('on');}
function setDuree(el,val){document.querySelectorAll('.dp').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('on'));el.classList.add('on');document.getElementById('preview-timer').textContent='Expire dans '+val;}
function updatePreview(){document.getElementById('preview-title').textContent=document.getElementById('pub-titre').value.trim()||'Votre titre apparaîtra ici';}
function ouvrirItineraire(){const p=PARTNERS.find(x=>x.id===window._ficheId);if(!p||!p.coords)return;window.open('https://www.google.com/maps/dir/?api=1&destination='+p.coords[0]+','+p.coords[1],'_blank');}
function startCounters(){let n=0,v=0;const t=setInterval(()=>{if(n<47)document.getElementById('cnt-n').textContent=++n;if(v<12)document.getElementById('cnt-v').textContent=++v;if(n>=47&&v>=12)clearInterval(t);},40);}
function initCarte(){
if(window._mapOk){window._map.invalidateSize();return;}
window._mapOk=true;
const map=L.map('map').setView([50.18,1.62],10);window._map=map;
L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png',{attribution:'© OpenStreetMap',maxZoom:18}).addTo(map);
const ico=(flash)=>L.divIcon({className:'',html:`<div style="width:${flash?32:26}px;height:${flash?32:26}px;background:${flash?'#C0392B':'#3D2B1F'};border:2px solid #FAF6F1;border-radius:50% 50% 50% 0;transform:rotate(-45deg);box-shadow:0 2px 4px rgba(0,0,0,.3)"></div>`,iconSize:[flash?32:26,flash?32:26],iconAnchor:[flash?16:13,flash?32:26],popupAnchor:[0,-30]});
PARTNERS.forEach(p=>{
if(!p.coords)return;
const popup=`<div style="font-family:sans-serif;min-width:160px;"><div style="font-weight:600;font-size:13px;color:#3D2B1F;margin-bottom:4px;">${p.name}</div>${p.flash?`<div style="background:#FDECEA;border:0.5px solid #C0392B;color:#7B1A1A;font-size:10px;padding:2px 6px;border-radius:4px;margin-bottom:4px;">FLASH · ${p.flash.titre}</div>`:''}<div style="font-size:11px;color:#8A6A50;margin-bottom:6px;">${p.avantage}</div><button onclick="showFiche(${p.id})" style="background:#3D2B1F;color:#FAF6F1;border:none;border-radius:6px;padding:5px 10px;font-size:11px;cursor:pointer;width:100%">Voir la fiche →</button></div>`;
L.marker(p.coords,{icon:ico(!!p.flash)}).addTo(map).bindPopup(popup);
});
setTimeout(()=>map.invalidateSize(),200);
}
renderList();
applyTranslations();
// Listeners boutons langue
document.querySelectorAll('.lang-btn').forEach(btn => {
btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
e.stopPropagation();
window.setLang(this.dataset.lang);
});
btn.addEventListener('touchend', function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
e.stopPropagation();
window.setLang(this.dataset.lang);
});
});
// Marquer le bon bouton de langue
document.querySelectorAll('.lang-btn').forEach(b => {
b.classList.toggle('on', b.dataset.lang === lang);
});
</script>
</body></html>
